24-28 Point Modern Decklists
============================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 7, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











Twenty players earned 24 point or more from their Modern rounds at Pro Tour *Oath of the Gatewatch*. Eleven hit exactly 24 points (8-2), three got to 25 points (8-1-1), four players received 27 points (9-1), and two skillful players (both in the Top 8) managed to run their records to 28 points (9-0-1) in the Modern rounds.




---

#### The following player finished with 28 points (9-0-1) in Modern:







#### Patrick Dickmann: Affinity


##### 




![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
